        end

        % Value changed function: x50_2
        function x50_2ValueChanged(app, event)
            f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
            value = app.x50_2.Value;
            if app.x50check2.Value == 1
                hold(app.RCFigure,"on")
                set(app.sss2,'visible','off')
                app.p2 = sigm_fit(app.bb2,app.aa2mean,[min(app.aa2mean) NaN value NaN],[]);
                xmso = linspace(min(app.bb2),max(app.bb2),100);
                y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p2,xmso);
                app.sss2 = plot(app.RCFigure,xmso,y_fit_mso,'b-','LineWidth',1);

                set(app.s1,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1)>4
                    set(app.sss1,'visible','on')
                    app.Sigmoid1.Value = 1;
                    app.Sigmoid1.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50_1.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50check1.Enable = 'on';
                elseif length(app.bb1)<=4
                    set(app.sss1, 'Visible','off')
                    app.Sigmoid1.Value = 0;
                    app.Sigmoid1.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50_1.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50check1.Enable = 'off';
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2)>4
                    set(app.sss2,'visible','on')
                    app.Sigmoid2.Value = 1;
                    app.Sigmoid2.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50_2.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50check2.Enable = 'on';
                elseif length(app.bb2)<=4
                    set(app.sss2, 'Visible','off')
                    app.Sigmoid2.Value = 0;
                    app.Sigmoid2.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50_2.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50check2.Enable = 'off';
                end
    
                hold(app.RCFigure,'off')
                legend(app.RCFigure,[app.s1,app.ss1,app.sss1,app.s2,app.ss2,app.sss2],{['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value)],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC'],['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value)],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC']});
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: ClearRC_SICIButton
        function ClearRC_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            delete(app.s1sp_SICI)
            delete(app.s2sp_SICI)
            delete(app.s1dp_SICI)
            delete(app.s2dp_SICI)
            app.s1sp_SICI = [];
            app.s2sp_SICI = [];
            app.s1dp_SICI = [];
            app.s2dp_SICI = [];
            delete(app.ss1sp_SICI)
            delete(app.ss2sp_SICI)
            delete(app.ss1dp_SICI)
            delete(app.ss2dp_SICI)
            app.ss1sp_SICI = [];
            app.ss2sp_SICI = [];
            app.ss1dp_SICI = [];
            app.ss2dp_SICI = [];
            delete(app.sss1sp_SICI)
            delete(app.sss2sp_SICI)
            delete(app.sss1dp_SICI)
            delete(app.sss2dp_SICI)
            app.sss1sp_SICI = [];
            app.sss2sp_SICI = [];
            app.sss1dp_SICI = [];
            app.sss2dp_SICI = [];
            set(app.RCFigure_SICI.Legend,'Visible','off')
            cla(app.RCFigure_SICI)
            app.RCtrialCollector1sp_SICI = [];
            app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI = 0;
            app.RCtrialCollector2sp_SICI = [];
            app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI = 0;
            app.RCtrialCollector1dp_SICI = [];
            app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI = 0;
            app.RCtrialCollector2dp_SICI = [];
            app.RCtrialCollector2dp_process_SICI = 0;
            app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Items = {'-'};
            app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Items = {'-'};
            app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Items = {'-'};
            app.RC2Ptsdp_SICI.Items = {'-'};
            app.MSOfloor_SICI = [0 100];
            app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim = [round(min(app.MSOfloor_SICI))-0.05*(max(app.MSOfloor_SICI)-min(app.MSOfloor_SICI)),round(max(app.MSOfloor_SICI))+0.05*(max(app.MSOfloor_SICI)-min(app.MSOfloor_SICI))];
            app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim = [0,1];
            app.rccounter1sp_SICI = repmat({0},1,100);
            app.rccounter2sp_SICI = repmat({0},1,100);
            app.rccounter1sp_all_SICI = 0;
            app.rccounter2sp_all_SICI = 0;
            app.rccounter1dp_SICI = repmat({0},1,100);
            app.rccounter2dp_SICI = repmat({0},1,100);
            app.rccounter1dp_all_SICI = 0;
            app.rccounter2dp_all_SICI = 0;
            app.onhold1sp_SICI = 0;
            app.onhold2sp_SICI = 0;
            app.onhold1dp_SICI = 0;
            app.onhold2dp_SICI = 0;
            s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,1,1]);
            addStyle(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",1:100);
            addStyle(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",1:100);
            addStyle(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI,s,"item",1:100);
            addStyle(app.RC2Ptsdp_SICI,s,"item",1:100);
            app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI = [];
            app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI = [];
            app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI = [];
            app.RCidx2dp_drop_SICI = [];
            app.RC1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.RC2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.RC1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.RC2sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.RC1dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.RC2dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.RC1dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.RC2dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.Sigmoid2sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.Sigmoid2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.Sigmoid1dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.Sigmoid2dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.Sigmoid1dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.Sigmoid2dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.bb1sp_SICI = [];
            app.aa1meansp_SICI = [];
            app.aa1stdsp_SICI = [];
            app.bb2sp_SICI = [];
            app.aa2meansp_SICI = [];
            app.aa2stdsp_SICI = [];
            app.bb1dp_SICI = [];
            app.aa1meandp_SICI = [];
            app.aa1stddp_SICI = [];
            app.bb2dp_SICI = [];
            app.aa2meandp_SICI = [];
            app.aa2stddp_SICI = [];
            app.x50_1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50_1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50_2sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50_2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50_1dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50_1dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50_2dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50_2dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50check1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50check2sp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50check2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50check1dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50check1dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            app.x50check2dp_SICI.Value = 0;
            app.x50check2dp_SICI.Enable = 'off';

            app.CurrentStim = 0;
            app.current_idx = 1;
            if app.InterpulseDurationCheck.Value == 0
                app.SICI_ICF_X = app.MSOEditField.Value;
                app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                xlabel(app.RCFigure_SICI, '%MSO')
                app.InterpulseCounter.Text = '-/-';
                app.SICI_ICF_state = '-';
            elseif app.InterpulseDurationCheck.Value == 1
                value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
                app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
                app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                xlabel(app.RCFigure_SICI, 'Interpulse Duration (ms)')
                app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
                app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
            end
            app.TopSP.Value = 0;
            app.TopDP.Value = 0;
            app.BotSP.Value = 0;
            app.BotDP.Value = 0;

            app.bin_SICI_ICF_X = [];
            app.bin_number = 0;
            app.bin_column = [];
            app.current_bin_number = 0;

            if app.TargetCh1.BackgroundColor == [0.07,0.62,1.00]
                app.TopSP.Value = 1;
                app.TopDP.Value = 1;
                app.BotSP.Value = 0;
                app.BotDP.Value = 0;
                app.Ch3Button_SICI.Value = 1;
            elseif app.TargetCh2.BackgroundColor == [0.07,0.62,1.00]
                app.TopSP.Value = 0;
                app.TopDP.Value = 0;
                app.BotSP.Value = 1;
                app.BotDP.Value = 1;
                app.Ch4Button_SICI.Value = 1;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: RC1sp_SICI
        function RC1sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.RC1sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: RC2sp_SICI
        function RC2sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.RC2sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: DropPtRC1sp_SICI
        function DropPtRC1sp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter1sp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,0,0]);
                addStyle(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI = [app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI,app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2)];
                
                app.RCidx1sp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter1sp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold1sp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold1sp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx1sp_SICI = app.RCidx1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI~=app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx1sp_SICI = app.RCidx1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI~=app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
                
                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                app.s1sp_SICI = scatter(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,1),app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),'ro','LineWidth',0.7);
                [aa1,app.bb1sp_SICI] = findgroups(app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,1));
                app.aa1meansp_SICI = splitapply(@median,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.aa1stdsp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.ss1sp_SICI = errorbar(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,app.aa1stdsp_SICI,'r*','LineWidth',1,'MarkerSize',18);

                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN app.x50_1sp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb1sp_SICI),max(app.bb1sp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p1sp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss1sp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'r-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Log #',app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,3));
                app.s1sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;
                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,4));
                app.s1sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;

                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
                legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                    {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC DP']});
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: DropPtRC2sp_SICI
        function DropPtRC2sp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter2sp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,0,0]);
                addStyle(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI = [app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI,app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2)];

                app.RCidx2sp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter2sp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold2sp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold2sp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx2sp_SICI = app.RCidx2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI~=app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx2sp_SICI = app.RCidx2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI~=app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                app.s2sp_SICI = scatter(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,1),app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),'bo','LineWidth',0.7);
                [aa2,app.bb2sp_SICI] = findgroups(app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,1));
                app.aa2meansp_SICI = splitapply(@median,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa2);
                app.aa2stdsp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa2);
                app.ss2sp_SICI = errorbar(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,app.aa2stdsp_SICI,'b*','LineWidth',1,'MarkerSize',18);
                
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check2sp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p2sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa2meansp_SICI) NaN app.x50_2sp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check2sp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p2sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa2meansp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb2sp_SICI),max(app.bb2sp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p2sp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss2sp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'b-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Log #',app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,3));
                app.s2sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;
                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,4));
                app.s2sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;

                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
                legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                    {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC DP']});
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: RecoverRC1sp_SICI
        function RecoverRC1sp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter1sp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,1,1]);
                addStyle(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI = app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI~=app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                
                app.RCidx1sp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter1sp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold1sp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold1sp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx1sp_SICI = app.RCidx1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI~=app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx1sp_SICI = app.RCidx1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI~=app.RCidx1sp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector1sp_SICI(app.RCidx1sp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
                
                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                app.s1sp_SICI = scatter(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,1),app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),'ro','LineWidth',0.7);
                [aa1,app.bb1sp_SICI] = findgroups(app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,1));
                app.aa1meansp_SICI = splitapply(@median,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.aa1stdsp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.ss1sp_SICI = errorbar(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,app.aa1stdsp_SICI,'r*','LineWidth',1,'MarkerSize',18);

                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN app.x50_1sp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb1sp_SICI),max(app.bb1sp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p1sp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss1sp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'r-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Log #',app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,3));
                app.s1sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;
                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector1sp_process_SICI(:,4));
                app.s1sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;

                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
                legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                    {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC DP']});
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: RecoverRC2sp_SICI
        function RecoverRC2sp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter2sp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,1,1]);
                addStyle(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                
                app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI = app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI~=app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));

                app.RCidx2sp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter2sp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold2sp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold2sp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx2sp_SICI = app.RCidx2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI~=app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx2sp_SICI = app.RCidx2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI~=app.RCidx2sp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector2sp_SICI(app.RCidx2sp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                app.s2sp_SICI = scatter(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,1),app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),'bo','LineWidth',0.7);
                [aa2,app.bb2sp_SICI] = findgroups(app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,1));
                app.aa2meansp_SICI = splitapply(@median,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa2);
                app.aa2stdsp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,2),aa2);
                app.ss2sp_SICI = errorbar(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,app.aa2stdsp_SICI,'b*','LineWidth',1,'MarkerSize',18);
                
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check2sp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p2sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa2meansp_SICI) NaN app.x50_2sp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check2sp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p2sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb2sp_SICI,app.aa2meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa2meansp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb2sp_SICI),max(app.bb2sp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p2sp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss2sp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'b-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Log #',app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,3));
                app.s2sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;
                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector2sp_process_SICI(:,4));
                app.s2sp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;

                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1

                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')

                    app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...

                    app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                    {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...

        % Value changed function: MeanStd1sp_SICI
        function MeanStd1sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: MeanStd2sp_SICI
        function MeanStd2sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: Sigmoid1sp_SICI
        function Sigmoid1sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                    app.x50_1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50check1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                    app.x50_1sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50check1sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: Sigmoid2sp_SICI
        function Sigmoid2sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.Sigmoid2sp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC2Ptssp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                    app.x50_2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                    app.x50check2sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                    app.x50_2sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                    app.x50check2sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: x50check1sp_SICI
        function x50check1sp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
            value = app.x50check1sp_SICI.Value;
            if value == 1
                app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN app.x50_1sp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
            elseif value == 0
                app.p1sp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1sp_SICI,app.aa1meansp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meansp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
            end
            hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
            set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            xmso = linspace(min(app.bb1sp_SICI),max(app.bb1sp_SICI),100);
            y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p1sp_SICI,xmso);
            app.sss1sp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'r-','LineWidth',1);

            set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                
            if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.RC2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
            legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...
                app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...
                ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC DP']});
        end

            set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')

            set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')

            set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
            set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')

            if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1

                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')

            if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Value = 1;
                app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                app.x50_1sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
                app.x50check1sp_SICI.Enable = 'on';
            elseif length(app.bb1sp_SICI)<=4 || app.TopSP.Value == 0
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Value = 0;
                app.Sigmoid1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                app.x50_1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
                app.x50check1sp_SICI.Enable = 'off';
            end

            if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
            end

            hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
            legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...

        % Button pushed function: RemoveLastButton
        function RemoveLastButtonPushed(app, event)
            app.GoodCount.Value = app.GoodCount.Value - 1;
            app.TotalCount.Value = app.TotalCount.Value - 1;
            GoodCountValueChanged(app, event)
            TotalCountValueChanged(app, event)
        end

        % Value changed function: InterpulseDurationCheck
        function InterpulseDurationCheckValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.InterpulseDurationCheck.Value;
            if value == 1
                xlabel(app.RCFigure_SICI, 'Interpulse Duration (ms)')
                if isempty(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value)
                    app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = '50';
                    app.SICI_ICF_X = 50;
                    app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                    app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/1'];
                elseif ~isempty(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value)
                    value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
                    app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
                    app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                    app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
                end
                app.ValueforCalculation.Enable = 'on';
                app.StartPercent_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.toLabel_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.EndPercent_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.byLabel_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.FloorPercent_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.Label_12.Enable = 'on';
                app.CalculateButton_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.RandomizeButton_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.orLabel.Enable = 'on';
                app.StartPercent_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.toLabel_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.EndPercent_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.byLabel_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.FloorPercent_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.CalculateButton_3.Enable = 'on';
                app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Enable = 'on';
                app.PrevButton.Enable = 'on';
                app.NextButton.Enable = 'on';
                app.Left1.Enable = 'on';
                app.Right1.Enable = 'on';
                app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
            elseif value == 0
                xlabel(app.RCFigure_SICI, '%MSO')
                app.SICI_ICF_X = app.MSOEditField.Value;
                app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                app.ValueforCalculation.Enable = 'off';
                app.StartPercent_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.toLabel_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.EndPercent_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.byLabel_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.FloorPercent_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.Label_12.Enable = 'off';
                app.CalculateButton_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.RandomizeButton_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.orLabel.Enable = 'off';
                app.StartPercent_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.toLabel_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.EndPercent_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.byLabel_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.FloorPercent_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.CalculateButton_3.Enable = 'off';
                app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Enable = 'off';
                app.PrevButton.Enable = 'off';
                app.NextButton.Enable = 'off';
                app.Left1.Enable = 'off';
                app.Right1.Enable = 'off';
                app.SICI_ICF_state = '-';
                app.InterpulseCounter.Text = '-/-';
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_2
        function CalculateButton_2Pushed(app, event)
            app.current_idx = 1;
            value = app.ValueforCalculation.Value*(app.StartPercent_2.Value:app.FloorPercent_2.Value:app.EndPercent_2.Value)/100;
            app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = num2str(value);
            value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
            app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
            app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
            app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
            app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
        end

        % Button pushed function: RandomizeButton_2
        function RandomizeButton_2Pushed(app, event)
            app.current_idx = 1;
            value = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
            Random_order = randperm(length(value));
            app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = num2str(value(Random_order));
            value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
            app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
            app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
            app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
            app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_3
        function CalculateButton_3Pushed(app, event)
            app.current_idx = 1;
            value = app.StartPercent_3.Value:app.FloorPercent_3.Value:app.EndPercent_3.Value;
            app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = num2str(value);
            value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
            app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
            app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
            app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
            app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
        end

        % Value changed function: Switch
        function SwitchValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.Switch.Value;
            if isequal(value,'SICI')
                app.current_task_value = 3;
            elseif isequal(value,'ICF')
                app.current_task_value = 4;
            end
        end

        % Value changed function: SelfDefinedRange_2
        function SelfDefinedRange_2ValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value;
            if isempty(value)
                app.current_idx = 1;
                app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = '50';
                app.SICI_ICF_X = 50;
                app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/1'];
            elseif ~isempty(value)
                value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
                try app.SICI_ICF_X = value2(app.current_idx);
                catch
                    app.current_idx = 1;
                    app.SICI_ICF_X = 50;
                    app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value = num2str(50);
                    app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/1'];
                end
                value2 = str2num(app.SelfDefinedRange_2.Value);
                app.InterpulseValue.Text = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
                app.InterpulseCounter.Text = [num2str(app.current_idx),'/',num2str(length(value2))];
            end
            app.SICI_ICF_state = num2str(app.SICI_ICF_X);
        end

        % Value changed function: RC1dp_SICI
        function RC1dp_SICIValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.RC1dp_SICI.Value;
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value,'-')
                if value == 0
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI, 'Visible','off')
                elseif value == 1
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI, 'Visible','on')
                end
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.XLim(2) + range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLimMode = 'auto';
                range = 0.05*(app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2)-app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1));
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(1) - range;
                app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) = app.RCFigure_SICI.YLim(2) + range;
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: DropPtRC1dp_SICI
        function DropPtRC1dp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter1dp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,0,0]);
                addStyle(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2));
                app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI = [app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI,app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2)];
                
                app.RCidx1dp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter1dp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold1dp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold1dp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx1dp_SICI = app.RCidx1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI~=app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx1dp_SICI = app.RCidx1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI~=app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
                
                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                app.s1dp_SICI = scatter(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,1),app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,2),'ko','LineWidth',0.7);
                [aa1,app.bb1dp_SICI] = findgroups(app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,1));
                app.aa1meandp_SICI = splitapply(@median,app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.aa1stddp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);
                app.ss1dp_SICI = errorbar(app.RCFigure_SICI,app.bb1dp_SICI,app.aa1meandp_SICI,app.aa1stddp_SICI,'k*','LineWidth',1,'MarkerSize',18);

                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check1dp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p1dp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1dp_SICI,app.aa1meandp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meandp_SICI) NaN app.x50_1dp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check1dp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p1dp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1dp_SICI,app.aa1meandp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meandp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb1dp_SICI),max(app.bb1dp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p1dp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss1dp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'k-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Log #',app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,3));
                app.s1dp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;
                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,4));
                app.s1dp_SICI.DataTipTemplate.DataTipRows(end+1) = row;

                set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.MeanStd2dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1sp_SICI)>4 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4 && app.TopDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2sp_SICI)>4 && app.BotSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if length(app.bb2dp_SICI)>4 && app.BotDP.Value == 1
                    set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
                legend(app.RCFigure_SICI,[app.s1sp_SICI,app.ss1sp_SICI,app.sss1sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s1dp_SICI,app.ss1dp_SICI,app.sss1dp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2sp_SICI,app.ss2sp_SICI,app.sss2sp_SICI, ...
                    app.s2dp_SICI,app.ss2dp_SICI,app.sss2dp_SICI], ...
                    {['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh1.Value),' RC DP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std SP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC SP'], ...
                    ['Channel ',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' mean+std DP'],['Ch',num2str(app.TargetCh2.Value),' RC DP']});
            end
        end

        % Button pushed function: RecoverRC1dp_SICI
        function RecoverRC1dp_SICIButtonPushed(app, event)
            if ~isequal(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Items{1},'-') && app.rccounter1dp_all_SICI>1
                s = uistyle("BackgroundColor",[1,1,1]);
                addStyle(app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI,s,"item",app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2));
                app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI = app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI~=app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2));
                
                app.RCidx1dp_SICI = 1:app.rccounter1dp_all_SICI;

                if app.onhold1dp_SICI == 0
                    app.onhold1dp_SICI = 1;
                    app.RCidx1dp_SICI = app.RCidx1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI~=app.RC1Ptsdp_SICI.Value(2));
                else
                    for i=1:length(app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI)
                        app.RCidx1dp_SICI = app.RCidx1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI~=app.RCidx1dp_drop_SICI(i));
                    end
                end
                app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI = app.RCtrialCollector1dp_SICI(app.RCidx1dp_SICI,:);

                f_sig = @(p,x) p(1) + (p(2)-p(1)) ./ (1 + 10.^((p(3)-x)*p(4)));
                
                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,"on")
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')

                app.aa1stddp_SICI = splitapply(@std,app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,2),aa1);

                if length(app.bb1dp_SICI)>4
                    if app.x50check1dp_SICI.Value == 1
                        app.p1dp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1dp_SICI,app.aa1meandp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meandp_SICI) NaN app.x50_1dp_SICI.Value NaN],[]);
                    elseif app.x50check1dp_SICI.Value == 0
                        app.p1dp_SICI = sigm_fit(app.bb1dp_SICI,app.aa1meandp_SICI,[min(app.aa1meandp_SICI) NaN NaN NaN],[]);
                    end
                    xmso = linspace(min(app.bb1dp_SICI),max(app.bb1dp_SICI),100);
                    y_fit_mso = f_sig(app.p1dp_SICI,xmso);
                    app.sss1dp_SICI = plot(app.RCFigure_SICI,xmso,y_fit_mso,'k-','LineWidth',1);
                end

                row = dataTipTextRow('Bin #',app.RCtrialCollector1dp_process_SICI(:,4));

                set(app.sss1sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2sp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss1dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.s2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.ss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                set(app.sss2dp_SICI,'visible','off')
                    
                if app.RC1sp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopSP.Value == 1
                    set(app.s1sp_SICI,'visible','on')
                end
    
                if app.RC1dp_SICI.Value == 1 && app.TopDP.Value == 1

                hold(app.RCFigure_SICI,'off')
